***разогревать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разогревать.html>разогрева́ть</a> (22722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>разо- + <a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>греть</a>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разогревать.html>разогрева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razogrevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разогреть.html>разогре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to warm up, to heat up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разогревать.html>разогрева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:публика.html>пу́блику</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razogrevátʹ</b> públiku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">warm/heat up the audience</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to reheat

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>греть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gretʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разогреть.html>разогре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razogrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разогревать.html>разогрева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to warm up, to heat up

<li>to reheat

<p><b>ра<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>гре́ть</a></b>

Зализняка — 12a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:разогревать.html>разогрева́ть</a>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ра<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зой<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́сь</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 7b/b⑨.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:расходиться.html>расходи́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>разо-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-й-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ти</b>; постфикс: <b>-сь</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a(1).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>разо-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-рв-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-нн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.

Зализняка — 1*a(2).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>разо-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-рв-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-нн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.

***разорвать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разорвать.html>разорва́ть</a> (3763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разорвать.html>разорва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razorvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрывать.html>разрыва́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tear apart/asunder, to tear up</li>
<li>to sever, to break (ties), to rend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to burst, to explode</li></ol>

***разорваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разорваться.html>разорва́ться</a> (10562)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разорвать.html>разорва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razorvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разорваться.html>разорва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razorvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрываться.html>разрыва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break, to tear, to burst</li>
<li>to burst, to go off, to explode</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to struggle to do (cope with) everything at once
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разорваться.html>разорва́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne móžet <b>razorvátʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he can't be everywhere at once</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***разорить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разорить.html>разори́ть</a> (9261)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">разорити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razoriti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orzoriti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orz-</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*oriti</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">разорити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razoriti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">разо̀рити</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">разорь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razorĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">орити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oriti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to destroy, to ravage</li>
<li>to ruin, to bring to ruin</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разорить.html>разори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разориться.html>разори́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razorítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разоряться.html>разоря́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ruin oneself, to come to ruin
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:покупка.html>поку́пки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разориться.html>разори́шься</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot takoj pokúpki ne <b>razoríšʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">such a purchase won't ruin you</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend money <i>(on)</i>, to fork out money <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">им <a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>пришло́сь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разориться.html>разори́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образование.html>образова́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">im prišlósʹ <b>razorítʹsja</b> na obrazovánije málʹčika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they had to fork out money for the boy's education</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разорить.html>разори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разорять.html>разоря́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razorjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разоряться.html>разоря́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razorjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разориться.html>разори́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ruin oneself, to come to ruin</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend money <i>(on)</i>, to fork out money <i>(for)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shout, to clamor, to make a din, to drone on, to drivel on, to nag <i>(at)</i>, to carp <i>(at)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тик</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разоряться.html>разоря́ется</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">opjátʹ étot polítik <b>razorjájetsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">that politician is drivelling on again!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разоряться.html>разоря́ться</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xvátit na menjá <b>razorjátʹsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stop nagging/shouting at me!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разорять.html>разоря́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razorjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
